    347 </a><a href="#h5-0-121" id="h5-0-121" class="i">+            &lt;p&gt;Hello, world! This is my first post ever made on this new site.&lt;/p&gt;
    348 </a><a href="#h5-0-122" id="h5-0-122" class="i">+&lt;p&gt;This is the place where Im going to write about my life, my work, and my hobbies. The things that I want to save in a secure place instead of my head.&lt;/p&gt;
    349 </a><a href="#h5-0-123" id="h5-0-123" class="i">+&lt;p&gt;Why am I making this website and not using some other tool like medium?&lt;br&gt;
    350 </a><a href="#h5-0-124" id="h5-0-124" class="i">+Well, the first reason is I dont know how to make a website so Im making this one.&lt;/p&gt;
    351 </a><a href="#h5-0-125" id="h5-0-125" class="i">+&lt;p&gt;The second reason is that I want control over the content of my posts and something very simple.&lt;br&gt;
    352 </a><a href="#h5-0-126" id="h5-0-126" class="i">+I dont want paywalls, ads, etc. Its just a blog, not a new NTF collection.&lt;/p&gt;
    353 </a><a href="#h5-0-127" id="h5-0-127" class="i">+&lt;p&gt;Well, maybe Ill add some ads in the future. &lt;strong&gt;Thats a bad joke&lt;/strong&gt; please ignore it.&lt;/p&gt;
    354 </a><a href="#h5-0-128" id="h5-0-128" class="i">+&lt;p&gt;The next post will be about how Im making this website and the resources Im using.&lt;/p&gt;
    355 </a><a href="#h5-0-129" id="h5-0-129" class="i">+&lt;p&gt;But if youre a little impatient, you can check out this &lt;a href=&quot;https://github.com/hectoraldairah/bitbyte-blog&quot;&gt;Github repo&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
    356 </a><a href="#h5-0-130" id="h5-0-130" class="i">+&lt;p&gt;Im using &lt;a href=&quot;https://www.11ty.dev/&quot;&gt;Eleventy&lt;/a&gt; btw.&lt;/p&gt;
    357 </a><a href="#h5-0-131" id="h5-0-131" class="i">+&lt;p&gt;Quote of the day:&lt;br&gt;
    358 </a><a href="#h5-0-132" id="h5-0-132" class="i">+You need to finish your shit before you start your next one.&lt;br&gt;
    359 </a><a href="#h5-0-133" id="h5-0-133" class="i">+- IDK&lt;/p&gt;
